  \n            </a>\n        \n    </h3>\n                    </div>\n                    \n                    \n                    \n                        \n                        \n                        <div class=\"card-lead\">\n                            <p>MONTREAL ­— If you were looking for a place to explore how the world has changed in the past half-century, you could do worse than venture here and contemplate the glory that was Expo 67, perhaps the greatest World’s Fair of the 20th century and certainly the most popular. </p>\n                        </div>\n
